<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">toilette</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">small cloth</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">toilette</i>.
</p>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:toilet.html>toilet</a></span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">room containing lavatory</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>; <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:men.html>men</a>'s room</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:ladies.html>ladies</a>' room</span>

<p>A frequentive verb derived from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">tokken</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-elen</i> (to pull, tap, tick).

<p>From Indonesian <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Malay_language" class="extiw" title="w:Malay language">Malay</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ms"><a href = vnd.unilang:toko.html>toko</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">shop</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Southern_Min" class="extiw" title="w:Southern Min"><a href = vnd.unilang:min.html>Min</a> Nan</a></span> <span class="Hani" lang="zh">土庫</span>／<span class="Hani" lang="zh">土库</span> (<i><span class="tr Latn">thó͘-khò͘</span></i>, “private storehouse”).

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:tolde.html>tolde</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">talde</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="ann-pos">first and third person singular preterite</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">tealde</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="ann-pos">first and third person singular preterite</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*talid-</i>, preterite <a href = vnd.unilang:stem.html>stem</a> of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*taljaną</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to count; tell</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">tell</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">-ed</i>.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">tolic</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh"><a href = vnd.unilang:tolk.html>tolk</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">тълкъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tŭlkŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">толкъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tolkŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*tъlkъ</i>.

***tollenaar.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tollenaar.html>tollenaar</a> (87274)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">tollenâer</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tol.html>tol</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-aar</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tollenaar.html>tollenaar</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tollenaars.html>tollenaars</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tollenaar.html>tollenaartje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A tax collector, in particular a collector of tolls; a publican.</li></ol>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The <a href = vnd.unilang:jack.html>jack</a> of trumps in the card game gleek.</li>

</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tom.html>tom</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:toms.html>toms</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> greengrocers'  <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A tomato <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">the fruit</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>.
<dl><dd><i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:toms.html>Toms</a></b> 90p a pound</i></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Rhyming <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a> from <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">tomfoolery</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tom.html>tom</a></strong> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:cockney.html>Cockney</a> rhyming <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> jewellery</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology 4</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">Uncle <a href = vnd.unilang:tom.html>Tom</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tom.html>tom</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:toms.html>toms</a></b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">tomming</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">tommed</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory<span class="ib-comma">,</span> of a black person</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To act in an obsequiously servile manner toward white authority.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_5">Etymology 5</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tom.html>tom</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:toms.html>toms</a></b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">tomming</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">tommed</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">nautical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To dig out a hole below the hatch cover of a bulker and fill it with cargo or weights to aid stability.</li></ol>
</body>

***tombola.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tombola.html>tombola</a> (53022)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it"><a href = vnd.unilang:tombola.html>tombola</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tombola.html>tombola</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">tombolas</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A lottery in which winning <a href = vnd.unilang:tickets.html>tickets</a> are drawn from a revolving drum.
<ul><li><b>1991</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Stephen_Fry" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Stephen Fry">Stephen Fry</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Liar_(novel)" class="extiw" title="w:The Liar (novel)">The Liar</a></i>, p. 60:
<dl><dd>He <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> given no choice in the matter of sharing <a href = vnd.unilang:rooms.html>rooms</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:gary.html>Gary</a> and he <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> drawn out of the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tombola.html>tombola</a></b> together, so together they <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

***tombstone.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tombstone.html>tombstone</a> (24366)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">tomb</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">stone</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tombstone.html>tombstone</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">tombstones</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A headstone marking a person's grave.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">headstone</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">gravestone</span></span></dd></dl>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1922</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Virginia_Woolf" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Virginia Woolf">Virginia Woolf</a>,  chapter 2, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jacob%27s_Room" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Jacob | s Room"><a href = vnd.unilang:jacob.html>Jacob</a>'s Room</a></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">True, there's no harm in <a href = vnd.unilang:crying.html>crying</a> for one's husband, and the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tombstone.html>tombstone</a></b>, though plain, <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> a solid piece of work, and on summer's days when the widow <a href = vnd.unilang:brought.html>brought</a> her boys to stand there one felt kindly towards her.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mathematics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The symbol "<i class="Zmth mention" lang="mul">∎</i>" marking the end of a proof.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">halmos</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">computing<span class="ib-comma">,</span> Microsoft <a href = vnd.unilang:windows.html>Windows</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A marker that <a href = vnd.unilang:takes.html>takes</a> the place of deleted data, allowing for replication of the deletion across <a href = vnd.unilang:servers.html>servers</a> etc.
<ul><li><b>2008</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:laura.html>Laura</a> E. Hunter, ‎Robbie <a href = vnd.unilang:allen.html>Allen</a>, <i>Active Directory Cookbook</i> (page 739)
<dl><dd>If you attempt to restore a backup that <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> older than the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tombstone.html>tombstone</a></b> lifetime, it may introduce <a href = vnd.unilang:objects.html>objects</a> that <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> deleted <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span></dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">computing</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A crashdump.
<ul><li><b>2014</b>, Joshua J. <a href = vnd.unilang:drake.html>Drake</a>, ‎Zach <a href = vnd.unilang:lanier.html>Lanier</a>, ‎Collin Mulliner, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:android.html>Android</a> Hacker's Handbook</i> (page 186)
<dl><dd>This actually results in a crash dump, which <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> written to the log and to a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tombstone.html>tombstone</a></b> file.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">cardiology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An unusual morphological feature on an electrocardiogram indicative of acute myocardial infarction, characterized by a massive ST elevation.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tombstone.html>tombstone</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">tombstones</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">tombstoning</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">tombstoned</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To take part in tombstoning: to jump into the sea, etc. from a <a href = vnd.unilang:cliff.html>cliff</a> or other high point so as to enter the water vertically straight.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">surfing</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> For a <a href = vnd.unilang:surfboard.html>surfboard</a> to stand upright half-submerged in the water (like a <a href = vnd.unilang:tombstone.html>tombstone</a>, above) because the surfer <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> underwater with his or her legrope pulled tight. Often this indicates a surfer in difficulty, either <a href = vnd.unilang:held.html>held</a> down by the power of a wave or unconscious and unable to get to the surface.
<ul><li><b>2005</b>, Bruce Jenkins, <i>Surfer</i> magazine, (referring to <a href = vnd.unilang:kelly.html>Kelly</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:slater.html>Slater</a>) <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://surfermag.com/features/events/mav05/">[1]</a>:
<dl><dd>Before the contest <a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a> started, <a href = vnd.unilang:slater.html>Slater</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:went.html>went</a> down hard in a warmup session. He <a href = vnd.unilang:took.html>took</a> a two-wave hold-down in the semifinals, his board <b>tombstoning</b> eerily for all to see, <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span></dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> computing<span class="ib-comma">,</span> Microsoft <a href = vnd.unilang:windows.html>Windows</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To replace (an object or data) with a <a href = vnd.unilang:tombstone.html>tombstone</a> marker.
<ul><li><b>2000</b>, William Boswell, <i>Inside <a href = vnd.unilang:windows.html>Windows</a> 2000 Server</i> (page 211)
<dl><dd>One of the many improvements in <a href = vnd.unilang:windows.html>Windows</a> 2000 WINS (and NT4 SP4) <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the capability to selectively delete or <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tombstone.html>tombstone</a></b> records.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
</body>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tomen.html>tomen</a> (58933)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">tômen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*tōmen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*taumijan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*taumijaną</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:toom.html>toom</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">briddle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.

***tone.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> tone (2816)</h1><br></body> 
***toneel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:toneel.html>toneel</a> (3935)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">tineel</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">tinel</i>; further origin uncertain. The modern Dutch term <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> adapted to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tonen.html>tonen</a></i> by folk etymology.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:toneel.html>toneel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:toneel.html>tonelen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:toneel.html>toneeltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>stage, scene, place for a performance in front of an assembled audience</li>
<li>scene, depiction on stage <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">often in the diminutive</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> or part of a performance</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">used absolutely, with definite article: <i><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:toneel.html>toneel</a></i></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">theatre</span>, the dramatical <a href = vnd.unilang:arts.html>arts</a>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:theater.html>theater</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> theatre, <span class="Latn" lang="en">site</span> where something (a crime, battle...) <a href = vnd.unilang:happens.html>happens</a>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:theater.html>theater</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">stage</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:podium.html>podium</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:planken.html>planken</a></span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">scene</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">scene</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">tableau-vivant</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tong.html>tong</a> (1937)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:tongen.html>tonge</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">tunga</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*tungǭ</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*dn̥ǵʰwéh₂s</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_6">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***tongs.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tongs.html>tongs</a> (112163)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:tong.html>tong</a> ("tool for manipulating <a href = vnd.unilang:things.html>things</a> in a fire") + -s
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tongs.html>tongs</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="plural number">pl</abbr></span> (<i>plural only</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>An instrument or tool used for picking <a href = vnd.unilang:things.html>things</a> up without touching them with the hands or <a href = vnd.unilang:fingers.html>fingers</a>, consisting of two slats or <a href = vnd.unilang:grips.html>grips</a> hinged at the end or in the middle, and sometimes including a spring to open the <a href = vnd.unilang:grips.html>grips</a>.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1977</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Agatha_Christie" class="extiw" title="w:Agatha Christie"><a href = vnd.unilang:agatha.html>Agatha</a> Christie</a>,  chapter 4, in  <cite>An Autobiography</cite>, part II, London |  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Collins,_Sons" class="extiw" title="w:William Collins, Sons">Collins</a>, <small>→ISBN</small>:</span><dl><dd></dd></dl></div>
<dl><dd>There <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> also hairdressing: hairdressing, too, really <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> hairdressing in those times — no running a comb through it and that <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> that. It <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> curled, frizzed, waved, put in curlers overnight, waved with hot <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tongs.html>tongs</a></b>;<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">by extension</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A large scissors-like two-piece center-hinged forged-iron implement with oval-loop handles and with pointed <a href = vnd.unilang:tips.html>tips</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:turned.html>turned</a> inward (in the same plane as and perpendicular to the handles) to facilitate lifting and carrying a block of ice. Often called ice <a href = vnd.unilang:tongs.html>tongs</a>.</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">ice <a href = vnd.unilang:tongs.html>tongs</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">pipe <a href = vnd.unilang:tongs.html>tongs</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">port <a href = vnd.unilang:tongs.html>tongs</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tongs.html>tongs</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">plural of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tong.html>tong</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">instrument</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*tōien</i>, variant of <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:touwen.html>touwen</a></i> (from which <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:touwen.html>touwen</a></i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*tawjaną</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tooien.html>tooien</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to adorn, decorate</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>

***toom.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:toom.html>toom</a> (78911)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*tōm</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*taumaz</i>.
Doublet with Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">team</i>, from English.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:toom.html>toom</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> or <abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tomen.html>tomen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:toom.html>toompje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>bridle, rein
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>Je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:moet.html>moet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:jongens.html>jongens</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:echt.html>echt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:toom.html>toom</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:houden.html>houden</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> You really need to keep those boys in check</dd></dl></li>
<li>a flock of <a href = vnd.unilang:birds.html>birds</a> (especially ducks, geese and <a href = vnd.unilang:swans.html>swans</a>)</li>
<li>frenulum</li></ol>

***toon.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:toon.html>toon</a> (1807)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_3">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:toon.html>toon</a></i>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">tonus</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_7">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:toon.html>toon</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tonen.html>tonen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:toontje.html>toontje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>tone</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms_2">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">grondtoon</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kiestoon.html>kiestoon</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">tonaal</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:toonhoogte.html>toonhoogte</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:toonladder.html>toonladder</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">sloottoon</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_3">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_8">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:toon.html>toon</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tonen.html>tonen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:toontje.html>toontje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dialectal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Dated form of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">teen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:toe.html>toe</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The front portion of a hoof.</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p>Still used in some dialects in <a href = vnd.unilang:utrecht.html>Utrecht</a> and Holland in the meaning “toe”. This variant seems to have <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> quite common in Hollandic dialects until the 19th century. Similar forms have also <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> found to exist in certain West Frisian and Dutch Low Saxon dialects.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>See the etymology of the main entry.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:toon.html>toon</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">first-person singular present indicative of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tonen.html>tonen</a></i></span></li>
<li><span class="use-with-mention">  imperative of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tonen.html>tonen</a></i></span></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tonen.html>tonen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to show</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beeld.html>beeld</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">image</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:toonbeeld.html>toonbeeld</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:toonbeelden.html>toonbeelden</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:toonbeeld.html>toonbeeldje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:paragon.html>paragon</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">model</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">example</span> to be followed or imitated <span class="defdate">[from late 17th c.]</span></li>
<li>An <span class="Latn" lang="en">imitation</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">reflection</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">sample</span>, illustration</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>(model) <span class="Latn" lang="nl">model</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:voorbeeld.html>voorbeeld</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span></li>
<li>(imitation) <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:navolging.html>navolging</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">evenbeeld</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span></li>
<li>(<a href = vnd.unilang:mannequin.html>mannequin</a>) <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:etalagepop.html>etalagepop</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:toon.html>toon</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">tone</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:soort.html>soort</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">type</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, rendering calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:modus.html>modus</a></i>.

***toothpick.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:toothpick.html>toothpick</a> (72394)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">tooth</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">pick</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:toothpick.html>toothpick</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">toothpicks</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A small, usually wooden, stick, often pointed at both <a href = vnd.unilang:ends.html>ends</a>, for removing food residue from between the teeth.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">dentiscalp</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">picktooth</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<div class="list-switcher" data-toggle-category="derived terms"><div class="derivedterms term-list ul-column-count" data-column-count="2" style="background-color: F8F8FF;">
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">HE-double-toothpicks</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">Missouri <a href = vnd.unilang:toothpick.html>toothpick</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">Texas <a href = vnd.unilang:toothpick.html>toothpick</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">toothpicker</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">toothpicklike</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">toothpickweed (<i>Visnaga daucoides</i>, syn. <i>Ammi visnaga</i>)</span></li></ul></div><div class="list-switcher-element" data-showtext=" show more ▼ " data-hidetext=" show less  " style="display: none;"> </div></div>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:toothpick.html>toothpick</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">toothpicks</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">toothpicking</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">toothpicked</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To spear (food) on a <a href = vnd.unilang:toothpick.html>toothpick</a>.</li>

***toque.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:toque.html>toque</a> (72387)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm"><a href = vnd.unilang:toque.html>toque</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:toque.html>toque</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arabic" class="extiw" title="w:Arabic">Arabic</a></span> <i class="Arab mention" lang="ar">طَاقِيَّة</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ar-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ṭāqiyya</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<div class="sister-wikipedia sister-project noprint floatright" style="border: 1px solid aaa; font-size: 90%; background: f9f9f9; width: 250px; padding: 4px; text-align: left;"><div style="float: left;"><div class="floatnone"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/44px-Wikipedia-logo.png" decoding="async" width="44" height="44" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/66px-Wikipedia-logo.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/88px-Wikipedia-logo.png 2x" data-file-width="200" data-file-height="200" /></div></div><div style="margin-left: 60px;">English Wikipedia <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> an article on:<div style="margin-left: 10px;"><b class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Toque_(French)" class="extiw" title="w:Toque (French)"><a href = vnd.unilang:toque.html>toque</a></a></b></div></div><span class="interProject"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Toque_(French)" class="extiw" title="w:Toque (French)">Wikipedia </a></span></div>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:toque.html>toque</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">toques</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A type of hat with no brim.
<ul><li><b>1903</b>—Janet Elder Rait, <i>Alison Howard</i>, Archibald Constable amp; Co., page 273,
<dl><dd>"Because Esmé <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a> she <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> going out this afternoon to choose a new <b><a href = vnd.unilang:toque.html>toque</a></b>, and she hoped I should like it, and I’m not quite sure what it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a>, or where she'<a href = vnd.unilang:ll.html>ll</a> wear it. Do you mind explaining?"</dd>
<dd>"Not at all. A <b><a href = vnd.unilang:toque.html>toque</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> that which if it <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:strings.html>strings</a> would be a bonnet, and if it <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> brim, would be a hat. It <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> worn on the head."</dd>
<dd>"<a href = vnd.unilang:thanks.html>Thanks</a>, now I know where I am," <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a> the vicar of St. Machars, with a sigh of relief.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1932</b>—Vyvyan Holland, translator, <i>The Strange River</i> by <a href = vnd.unilang:julien.html>Julien</a> Green, Harper amp; Brothers, page 180,
<dl><dd>She <a href = vnd.unilang:drank.html>drank</a> a glass of wine mixed with water, <a href = vnd.unilang:took.html>took</a> off her felt <b><a href = vnd.unilang:toque.html>toque</a></b> and her <a href = vnd.unilang:shoes.html>shoes</a>, and slid beneath the red eiderdown.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1957</b>—<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Samuel_Beckett" class="extiw" title="w:Samuel Beckett">Samuel Beckett</a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Endgame_(play)" class="extiw" title="w:Endgame (play)">"<a href = vnd.unilang:endgame.html>Endgame</a>"</a>,
<dl><dd>In a dressing-gown, a stiff <b><a href = vnd.unilang:toque.html>toque</a></b> on his head, a large blood-stained handkerchief <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> his face, a whistle hanging from his neck, a <a href = vnd.unilang:rug.html>rug</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> his knees, thick <a href = vnd.unilang:socks.html>socks</a> on his <a href = vnd.unilang:feet.html>feet</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:hamm.html>Hamm</a> seems to be asleep.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">specifically</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A tall white hat with no brim of the sort worn by <a href = vnd.unilang:chefs.html>chefs</a>
<ul><li><b>1999</b>—Michael Ruhlman, <i>The Making of a <a href = vnd.unilang:chef.html>Chef</a>: Mastering Heat at the Culinary Institute of America</i>, Owl Books, →ISBN, page 154,
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:chef.html>Chef</a> Felder <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> in her early forties, slender, with short wavy brown hair, almost all of which could be contained within her <b><a href = vnd.unilang:toque.html>toque</a></b>.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2000</b>—Jerrilyn Farmer, <i>Killer Wedding</i>, HarperCollins, →ISBN, page 103,
<dl><dd>When I <a href = vnd.unilang:came.html>came</a> to the back of a <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a>'s head, wearing a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:toque.html>toque</a></b>, I <a href = vnd.unilang:knew.html>knew</a> I'd spotted my quarry.</dd>
<dd>"<a href = vnd.unilang:chef.html>Chef</a> Reynoso?"</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2004</b>—Laura Levine, <i>Killer <a href = vnd.unilang:blonde.html>Blonde</a></i>, Kensington Books, →ISBN, page 114,
<dl><dd>Minutes <a href = vnd.unilang:later.html>later</a>, a red-faced <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a> in a <a href = vnd.unilang:chef.html>chef</a>'s <b><a href = vnd.unilang:toque.html>toque</a></b> approached our table.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">by extension<span class="ib-comma">,</span> informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <a href = vnd.unilang:chef.html>chef</a>.
<ul><li><b>2007</b>—October, Nicole Berrie, "Green Eggs and <a href = vnd.unilang:sam.html>Sam</a>", in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Elle" class="extiw" title="w:Elle"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:elle.html>Elle</a></i></a>, page 360,
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:sam.html>Sam</a> Mason first grabbed the spotlight as the pastry <a href = vnd.unilang:chef.html>chef</a> ... for being the most rock 'n' roll <b><a href = vnd.unilang:toque.html>toque</a></b> in town.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>A variety of bonnet monkey; <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/toque_macaque" class="extiw" title="w:toque macaque"><a href = vnd.unilang:toque.html>toque</a> macaque</a>, <span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Macaca_sinica" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Macaca sinica"><i>Macaca sinica</i></a></span>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An African nominal money of account, equal to 40 cowries.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>1871. Assimilated from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Canadian_French" class="extiw" title="w:Canadian French">Canadian French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">tuque</i>. Likely to be an hypercorrection from the time that <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:toque.html>toque</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> already in the dictionaries when they didn'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> yet list <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">tuque</i> as a <a href = vnd.unilang:kind.html>kind</a> of hat. French word <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">tuque</i> for hat <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> itself not strictly a deformation of French <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:toque.html>toque</a></i> : it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> also related to other meanings of <i>tuque</i> and to its former name <i>bonnet à la turque</i> (<a href = vnd.unilang:lit.html>lit</a>. Turkish-style bunnet/cap).
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<div class="sister-wikipedia sister-project noprint floatright" style="border: 1px solid aaa; font-size: 90%; background: f9f9f9; width: 250px; padding: 4px; text-align: left;"><div style="float: left;"><div class="floatnone"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/44px-Wikipedia-logo.png" decoding="async" width="44" height="44" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/66px-Wikipedia-logo.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/88px-Wikipedia-logo.png 2x" data-file-width="200" data-file-height="200" /></div></div><div style="margin-left: 60px;">English Wikipedia <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> an article on:<div style="margin-left: 10px;"><b class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tuque" class="extiw" title="w:Tuque">Tuque</a></b></div></div><span class="interProject"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tuque" class="extiw" title="w:Tuque">Wikipedia </a></span></div>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:toque.html>toque</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">toques</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Canada" class="extiw" title="w:Canada">Canada</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A knitted hat, usually conical but of varying shape, often woollen, and sometimes topped by a pom-pom or tassel.
<ul><li><b>1998</b>, Douglas Coupland, <i>Girlfriend in a <a href = vnd.unilang:coma.html>Coma</a></i>, ch 1:
<dl><dd>Such <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the demented nature of the universe that I <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> too weak to properly respond to my being hit on by carloads of Betties and Veronicas—all except for the cheeky Cheryl Anderson who <a href = vnd.unilang:gave.html>gave</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> ‘manual release’ the day I <a href = vnd.unilang:lost.html>lost</a> my eye-brows, followed by a flood of <a href = vnd.unilang:tears.html>tears</a> and the snapping of <a href = vnd.unilang:polaroids.html>Polaroids</a> in which I wear a knit <b><a href = vnd.unilang:toque.html>toque</a></b>. Gush gush.</dd></dl></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2018</b> March,  <a href = vnd.unilang:laura.html>Laura</a> Bliss,  “How WeWork <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>Has</a> Perfectly Captured the Millennial Id”, in  <cite>The Atlantic</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://www.theatlantic.com/magazine/archive/2018/03/wework-the-perfect-manifestation-of-the-millennial-id/550922/">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">It <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> like entering the Millennial id. Craft <a href = vnd.unilang:beer.html>beer</a> and cucumber water poured from kitchen <a href = vnd.unilang:taps.html>taps</a>. Laptoppers in <a href = vnd.unilang:jeans.html>jeans</a> and <b>toques</b> clacked along to MGMT in the wood-paneled common area.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:beanie.html>beanie</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">knit cap</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">stocking cap</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">watch cap</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spanish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Spanish language">Spanish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="es"><a href = vnd.unilang:toque.html>toque</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:toque.html>toque</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">toques</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">music</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A rhythm used in Latin music, especially Cuban religious rituals.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">music</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The guitar part of <a href = vnd.unilang:flamenco.html>flamenco</a> music.</li></ol>

</p>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">torre</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">turn</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">tur</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">turris</i>.
